 2014 ke chunaav main congress loksabhaa main sabase badi vipakshi party thi, jiske paas kul 44 sadsy the
 The Congress was not authorized to be the Leader of the Opposition on the basis of not having at least 55 members in 545 i
e
 10% of the total seats of the Lok Sabha
 is baar satrahavin loksabhaa main congress ne ghoshnaa kar di he ki uske paas kul 52 sadsy hai jo 10 fisadi kii shart puri nahin karte, isliye vah netaa pratipaksh kaa pad nahin maangegi
 It is extremely important that before the formation of the next Lok Sabha, legal arguments are being presented in favor or opposition of the Leader of the Opposition
 netaa pratipaksh ke 10 pratishat kii shart kaise ai?2014 main congress ko netaa pratipaksh kaa pad dene ke bare main loksabhaa spikar ne centre sarkaar ke sarvocch kanoonee adhikari atarni general mukul rohtagi se salaah lee thi
 The advice given by Mukul Rohatgi on 23 July 2014 had three main points
 pehla, rohtagi ne 1956 main loksabhaa spikar ke nirdesh 120 or 121(1)(c) kaa hawala diya
 This directive states that if a party does not meet the quorum of having 10 per cent of the total members of the Lok Sabha, then the Speaker of the Lok Sabha is not bound to recognize the leader of the largest opposition party as the Leader of the Opposition
 haalanki, nirdesh 120 kahata he ki loksabhaa adhyaksh sadan kii prakriya ko sucharu rup se chalaane ke makasad se sadasyon ke ek association ko sansadeey dal yaa samooh ke rup main manyata de saktaa he or loksabhaa adhyaksh kaa nirnay antim hoga
 Directive 121 (1) (c) states that at least the prescribed quorum must be fulfilled to give recognition to the Parliamentary Party which constitutes 10 per cent of the total members of the House
 in nirdeshon main netaa pratipaksh kaa koi zikr nahin he, jabaki yah sansadeey dal yaa samooh kii manyata dene kii baat karata he
 What was the purpose of these directives of 1956
 Instruction 122 mentions 7 objectives: (a) Allotment of seats and blocks in the house (b) Allotment of rooms in Parliament House (c) Allotting committee room for party meeting (d) ) Supplying official documents (e) Nominating for parliamentary committees (f) Handing out a panel of names to the speaker for debate (g) Getting advice for moving the House or discussing any important points that come up in the House
 rohtagi kaa doosraa tark tha ki netaa pratipaksh kii manyata 'selleri and elounsej of leader of apojishan in parliament act, 1977' ke daayre main nahin aati he, jabaki netaa pratipaksh ke liye jo bhi naam saamne aata he, 'selleri and elounsej aaf leader aaf apojishan in parliament act, 1977' use sanvaidhanik manyata detaa he or yah pehali baar tha jab netaa pratipaksh pad ko kanoonee taur par vyakhyayit kiya gaya
 Section 2 of the law says that the speaker who will be the largest party in opposition in the lower house i
e
 Lok Sabha, will recognize its leader as the leader of the opposition, but there is no mention of the condition of having at least 10 percent of the members, on the basis of which Leader of the Opposition should be elected
 haalanki, rohtagi kaa tark he ki 1977 ke vidheyak ke paas hone ke baad bhi saatvin loksabhaa main netaa pratipaksh kaa pad khaali hi rahaa
 In 1956, the Speaker's directive to the Leader of the Opposition remained effective
 2005 se 2010 tak loksabhaa ke mahasachiv rahe pediti acharya kaa vichaar alag he
 He says that after the coming of 'salary and Alliances of Leaders of Opposition in Parliament Act, 1977', the post of Leader of Opposition got constitutional status and it was established
 is vidheyak ke paas hone ke baad 1956 kaa spikar kaa nirdesh apraasangik ho gaya
 After the 10th Schedule came into effect in 1985 (anti-defection Law), importance is given to every opposition party irrespective of the member numbers
 10veen anusuchee ne spikar ke nirdesh 120 ko apraasangik bana diya

 ve kehete hai ki 1977 kaa act yaa koi doosraa kanoon yah nahin kahata he ki spikar kaa nirdesh avaidhanik he, lekin ve yah bhi kehete hai ki spikar ko netaa pratipaksh kii manyata deni chahie, kyonki yah ek jimmedaari kaa pad he or swasth loktantr ke liye jaruri he ki majboot sarkaar ke khilaaf ek sthaayee vipaksh bhi ho
 Rohatgi's third argument was about the presence of the Leader of Opposition in the selection committees formed under the CVC Act, RTI Act, Lokpal and Lokayukta Act and Human Rights Act
 unhone kaha ki sivisi act or artiai act main loksabhaa ke netaa pratipaksh ke vikalp ke rup main sabase badi party ke netaa kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 These four laws also provide that even if a post is vacant in the selection committee, the selection made by it will not be illegal, so Rohatgi denied the statutory requirement of the Leader of Opposition
 aage kya ho?yah myne nahin rakhata ki kanoonee bahes koun jeet rahaa he
 The Leader of Opposition has its own importance for effective opposition in Parliament
 iske alaava sivisi, sibiai, siaisi, lokapal jaisi javabdeh sansthaaon kii niyuktiyon main nishpakshta or paardarshita banaae rakhane ke liye bhi netaa pratipaksh kaa hona behad jaruri he
 Nor should it be exaggerated, nor should it be viewed inferiorly
 yah mahatv nahin rakhata ki kanoon main kitna jhol yaa kitni aspashtataa he, jaisaa ki rohtagi ne pesh kii thi

 Apart from this, the job of the Leader of Opposition in formulating policies and legislative work in the House is to unite the opposition and to keep it effective

 Pregnancy is a time when a pregnant woman goes through many physical and mental changes
 ek ore jahaan use khud ko aane vaale jivan ke liye taiyaar karnaa padataa vahiin kai shaareerik badlaavon ko bhi sahan karnaa padataa he
 These changes have a bearing on the behavior of the woman as well as her organs
 is dauraan mahila ko har roj kisi na kisi tarah kii pareshaani se guzarana padataa he lekin sharir ke kuch khaas angon main dard hona sabase takalifdeh hota he
 During this time, some parts of the body often have pain: 1
 peeth main dard honise dauraan peeth main dard hona bahut aam he
 This happens because the uterus is growing in the womb, which makes the front part very heavy
 pet baari ho jane kii vajah sepith main jhukaav aana shuru ho jaataa he
 This causes pain in the back almost daily
 2
 Feet pain: During pregnancy, the upper body weight of the woman increases significantly
 jisase uske pairon par bahut adhik bhaar padane lagata he
 The bones are not able to bear this weight and because of this, there is always pain in the legs
 3
 Headache: There is heaviness in the head every morning during pregnancy
 iskaa pramukh kaaran ye bhi hota he ki is dauraan neend aniyamit ho jaati he
 In such a situation, headaches often occur due to lack of sleep and hormonal changes
 4
 Pain in the breast During this time, many hormonal changes occur due to which the breasts become big and hard
 jisaki vajah seunamem aksar dard bana rahata he
 5
 pet dardeshishu ke vikaas ke saath-saath mahila ko acidity kii samasya shuru ho jaati he
 Due to which nausea, stomach pain also persists

 This is the first meeting of the BJP National Council after Narendra Modi became Prime Minister
 isamen bataur bijepi adhyaksh amit shah ke naam par muhar lagi
 Former BJP president Rajnath Singh approved the name of Amit Shah, which was approved by the National Council of BJP

 kaveri jal vivaad par supreme court ne apana faisla suna diya he

 kaveri jal vivaad tribunel ne is masale par 5 farvari ko apana antim aadesh diya tha, jise karnataka or tamilnadu donon rajyon ne supreme court main chunauti di thi
 Kaveri is also called Ganga of South India
 yah pashchimi ghat ke parvat brahmagiri se nikali he
 Its length is about 800 kilometers
 kaveri nadi ke delta par acchhee kheti hoti he
 There is a dispute between the two states regarding its water
 supreme court ne kaaphi lambii sunwaayee ke baad pichley saal 20 sitambar ko apana faisla surakshit rakh liya tha
 This is a very emotional issue for millions of families dependent on the waters of this river in Karnataka and Tamil Nadu
 aaie 10 binduon main jaanate hai ki aakhir kya he yah vivaad
 
 
 1
 kaveri nadi jal ke vitaran or istemaal par karnataka or tamilnadu ke ilaake ke logon ke bich kareeb 137 saal se vivaad chal rahaa he
 The dispute first arose in 1881 when the erstwhile Mysore state decided to build a dam on the Kaveri
 tatkaaleen madras rajya ne is par aapatti kii
 After the mediation of the British people, an agreement was reached on this in 1924, after many years
 lekin vivaad aazaadee ke pehle or aazaadee ke baad bhi jari rahaa
 2
 saal 1990 main kaveri jal vivaad tribunel (CWDT) kii sthapana hui
 In 2007, the tribunal placed its order on it
 lekin supreme court ke aadesh ke baad hi saal 2013 main centre sarkaar ne is aadesh se sambandhit adhisuchana jari kii
 3
 kaveri nadi ke jal par chaar rajyon ke karodon log nirbhar hai
 The tribunal, in its order, allocated 419 teamac feet to Tamil Nadu, 270 teamac feet to Karnataka, 30 TMC feet to Kerala (a tributary of Kaveri passes through the state) and 7 TMC feet to Puducherry
 4
 The Cauvery Tribunal, based on 100 years of average water availability in the river, estimated that even if half of its water is available for use, 740 feet of TMC water can be found
 tribnunal ne karnataka ko aadesh diya ki use june se lekar may tak har saal 192 tiemasi foot pani chhodana hoga
 5
 tribunel ne kaha ki kharaab monsoon vaale saal main sabhi rajyon ko isi anupaat main jal main kami ko saajha karnaa hoga
 But this provision further increased the dispute between Karnataka and Tamil Nadu
 6
 In the last few years, due to erratic monsoon and huge water crisis in Bengaluru, Karnataka has been repeatedly saying that it does not have enough water in the Cauvery river basin to give Tamil Nadu its share
 7
 On the other hand, Tamil Nadu was also not happy with the Cauvery tribunal's order
 agast 2016 main tamilnadu supreme court kii sharan main chalaa gaya, yah daawa karte hue ki tribunel kaa aadesh galat he, kyonki usne sirf fasal ke mausam kaa dhyaan rakhaa he
 8
 tamilnadu kaa tark he ki rajya ke kisaan saal main do fasal bote hai, isliye unhen karnataka ke mukaable zyada pani milanaa chahie
 Tamil Nadu also argues that they need more water than the allocation of tribunals, as Samba paddy is cultivated in the state, which requires more water
 9
 Following this move by the Tamil Nadu government, Karnataka also immediately moved the Supreme Court and demanded additional water for the state
 karnataka ne kaha ki monsoon main utaar-chadhaav aurakam barish kiwajah se uske liye yah sambhav nahin he ki tribnul dwaara tamilnadu ke liye tay aavanton se zyada pani chhod sake
 10
 sitambar 2016 main supreme court ne karnataka ko aadesh diya ki vah agle 10 dinon ke liye har dinatamilnadu cocaveri nadi kaa 15,000 kusek pani de

 vinamr shradhanjali! Lord Shiva soon becomes pleased with his devotees
 bholenath ko unki saumy akruti ke saath unke raudrarupa ke liye pahachaanaa jaataa he
 According to the Vedas, the devotee follows Shiva Chalisa to overcome the difficulties and obstacles of his life
 shiv chalisa ke madhyam se aap bhi apane dukhon ko dur karke shiv kii apaar krupa praapt kar sakate hai
 Shiva Chalisa has great importance in a person's life
 shiv chalisa ke saral shabdon se bhagwaan shiv ko aasaani se prasann kiya ja saktaa he
 The most difficult task can be done very easily with the recitation of Shiva Chalisa
 shiv chalisa kii 40 panktiyaan saral shabdon main vidyaman he jinaki mahima bahut hi zyada he
 Lord Shiva is called Bholenath because of his naive nature
 unki shiv chalisa kaa paath karne se wo apane kisi bhi bhakt se aasaani se maan jate hai or unhen manachaaha vardaan de dete hai
 What is the simple method of reciting Shiva Chalisa - wake up early in the morning and take a bath and wear clean clothes
 - apana munh purv disha main rakhen or kusha ke asana par baithe
 In worship, white garland, rice, kalava, incense-deep yellow flower garland and if possible, keep 11 flowers of white mud and keep pure mishri for offerings
 - paath karne se pehle gaay ke ghi kaa diya jalaaen or ek lote main shuddh jal bharkar rakhen
 - Recite Lord Shiva's Shivchalisa three or five times
 - shiv chalisa kaa paath bol bolkar karen jitne logon ko yah sunai degaa unako bhi laabh hoga
 - Read Shiv Chalisa with full devotion and please Lord Shiva
 -paath puraa ho jane par lote kaa jal saare ghar me chhidak den
 - Drink a little water on your own and eat it as Mishri Prasad and distribute it among the children
